</header><div class="entry-content"><div class="tasty-pins-hidden-image-container" style="display:none;"><img alt="Glass of almond milk beside a plate of gluten-free Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies" class="tasty-pins-hidden-image" data-pin-description="EASY 1-Bowl Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies! <p>Peanut butter cookies seem so effortless. Just throw peanut butter and some other random ingredients in your kitchen into a bowl, bake, and <em>voila!</em> — peanut butter cookies! Or so I thought.</p>
<p>This recipe was tested and retested and scrapped and tested again. It caused us so much trouble, but we’re happy to report we stuck with it and are <em>so</em> happy with the results.</p>
<iframe allow="accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="380" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Mn8Avk77nRE" width="680"></iframe>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Oats, brown sugar, gluten-free four, natural peanut butter, egg, and other ingredients for making our Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies recipe" class="wp-image-49877" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Healthier Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies (GF &amp; 1 Bowl!)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/healthier-peanut-butter-chocolate-chip-cookies-gf-1-bowl/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe.jpg" data-pin-description="EASY 1-Bowl Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies! SALTY-SWEET, PERFECT texture! #minimalistbaker #peanutbutter #glutenfree #cookie #glutenfree #recipe" data-pin-title="Healthier Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies (GF &amp; 1 Bowl!)" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-217x300.jpg 217w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-768x1060.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-742x1024.jpg 742w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-600x828.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-680x939.jpg 680w"/></figure>
<span id="more-49841"></span>
<p>Thanks to a little inspo from the talented <a aria-label="Liz Moody (opens in a new tab)" href="https://www.lizmoody.com/best-healthy-cookies/" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow" target="_blank">Liz Moody</a>, we finally got the perfect base formula right, and it’s <strong>butter- and oil-free</strong>!</p>
<p>The problem with our previous attempts was adding fat in addition to the peanut butter, or adding too many dry ingredients, or too many wet ingredients. Friends, it was touch and go. But this <strong>simple, unfussy, 1-bowl technique</strong> is perfection!</p>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Using a wooden spoon to stir gluten-free Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookie batter" class="wp-image-49864" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Healthier Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies (GF &amp; 1 Bowl!)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/healthier-peanut-butter-chocolate-chip-cookies-gf-1-bowl/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-5.jpg" data-pin-description="EASY 1-Bowl Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies! SALTY-SWEET, PERFECT texture! #minimalistbaker #peanutbutter #glutenfree #cookie #glutenfree #recipe" data-pin-title="Healthier Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies (GF &amp; 1 Bowl!)" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-5.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-5.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-5-217x300.jpg 217w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-5-768x1062.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-5-741x1024.jpg 741w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-5-600x830.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-5-680x940.jpg 680w"/></figure>
<p>Simply stir dry ingredients: brown sugar, gluten-free flour, rolled oats, salt, and baking powder.</p>
<p>Then add wet ingredients: peanut butter, egg, vanilla. And stir again. Throw in some chocolate chips and you’re good to go! <strong>No chilling required!</strong></p>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Chocolate chips in a bowl of gluten-free Peanut Butter Cookie batter" class="wp-image-49866" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Healthier Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies (GF &amp; 1 Bowl!)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/healthier-peanut-butter-chocolate-chip-cookies-gf-1-bowl/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-7.jpg" data-pin-description="EASY 1-Bowl Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies! SALTY-SWEET, PERFECT texture! #minimalistbaker #peanutbutter #glutenfree #cookie #glutenfree #recipe" data-pin-title="Healthier Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies (GF &amp; 1 Bowl!)" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-7.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-7.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-7-213x300.jpg 213w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-7-768x1081.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-7-727x1024.jpg 727w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-7-600x845.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-7-680x957.jpg 680w"/></figure>
<p>This batter comes together in less than 10 minutes. Baking is just another 10 minutes. That means cookies that are <strong>ready in like 20 minutes</strong>!</p>
<p>Faster cookies = better cookies. It’s science.</p>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Baking sheet of unbaked Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies" class="wp-image-49868" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Healthier Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies (GF &amp; 1 Bowl!)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/healthier-peanut-butter-chocolate-chip-cookies-gf-1-bowl/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/EASY-1-Bowl-Peanut-Butter-Chocolate-Chip-Cookies-SALTY-SWEET-PERFECT-texture-minimalistbaker-peanutbutter-glutenfree-cookie-glutenfree-recipe-10.jpg" data-pin-description="EASY 1-Bowl Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies! <p>We hope you LOVE these cookies! They’re:</p>
<p>Peanut buttery<br/>Salty-sweet<br/>Tender with a slight chew<br/>Studded with chocolate<br/>&amp; Incredibly delicious</p>
<p>These would make the perfect treat to have on hand throughout the week. They also keep well in the freezer for when sweet cravings strike!</p>

<h2 class="wprm-recipe-name">Healthier Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies (GF &amp; 1 Bowl!)</h2>
<div class="wprm-recipe-summary">
<p>Healthier 1-Bowl Peanut Butter Chocolate Chip Cookies made without butter or oil. Perfectly chewy, salty-sweet, and studded with chocolate chips!</p> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-author-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-author-name">Author:</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-author">Minimalist Baker</span>
</div>
</div>

<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredients-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Ingredients</h3>
<div class="wprm-unit-conversion-container"><a class="wprm-unit-conversion wprmpuc-active" data-recipe="49907" data-system="1" href="#">US Customary</a> – <a class="wprm-unit-conversion" data-recipe="49907" data-system="2" href="#">Metric</a></div> <div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">rolled oats</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(ensure gluten-free friendly as needed)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/diy-gluten-free-flour-blend/" target="_blank">gluten-free flour </a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub other flour, such as almond or unbleached all-purpose)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">sea salt </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(plus more for topping)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">baking powder</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">brown sugar </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or try subbing coconut sugar, but we only tested with brown)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">creamy salted peanut butter </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(we like Wild Friends — ingredients should only be peanuts and salt)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">vanilla extract</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">large</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">egg</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(organic, pasture-raised when possible)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">dark chocolate chips (dairy-free), chopped </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(plus more for topping)</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Instructions</h3>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group">
<ol class="wprm-recipe-instructions">
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Preheat oven to 350 degrees F (176 C) and line a large baking sheet with parchment paper.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>To a medium mixing bowl, add gluten-free oats, gluten-free flour blend, sea salt, baking powder, and brown sugar and whisk to combine.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Add peanut butter (ensure it’s natural and pourable — just peanuts and salt), vanilla, and egg and stir until a tacky dough is formed. Depending on the freshness / drippiness of your peanut butter, you may need to add a little more GF flour if it’s too wet. Or, if it’s too dry or crumbly, compensate with a bit more peanut butter (or a splash of dairy-free milk). We found ours didn't need any adjustments.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Stir in chocolate chips. Then scoop out dough in 1 ½ Tbsp amounts (I like using <a href="https://aax-us-east.amazon-adsystem.com/x/c/Qvk8AodUlhizL_NsgsD3UYkAAAFnDsOoEAEAAAFKAWrSURY/https://www.amazon.com/dp/B016QDV7GK/ref=as_at?creativeASIN=B016QDV7GK&amp;linkCode=w61&amp;imprToken=StvX2934fT6nZ50UCV6PhQ&amp;slotNum=27&amp;tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="nofollow" target="_blank"><em>this scoop</em></a>) and place on prepared baking sheet. Top with another sprinkle of chocolate chips and press down slightly to form into a disc shape.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Bake for 10-12 minutes, or until the edges appear slightly golden brown and they’ve expanded to about twice their original size. Remove from oven and let cool on pan for 10 minutes (top with another small sprinkle of salt at this time – <em>optional</em>). Then enjoy (preferably with <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/guide-making-dairy-free-milk/" target="_blank">dairy-free milk</a>).</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Store cookies well sealed at room temperature up to 4-5 days, in the refrigerator up to 1 week, or in the freezer up to 1 month (let thaw before enjoying).</div>
</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-video-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header"></h3>
<iframe allow="accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="380" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Mn8Avk77nRE" width="680"></iframe> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-notes-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Notes</h3>
<p>*Nutrition information is a rough estimate.<br>*Recipe adapted from <a href="https://www.lizmoody.com/best-healthy-cookies/" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank">Liz Moody</a>.</br></p>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-nutrition-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Nutrition Per Serving (1 of 12 cookies) </h3><ul><li><strong>Calories:</strong> 129 <li><strong>Fat:</strong> 7.4g <li><strong>Saturated fat:</strong> 1.9g <li><strong>Polyunsaturated fat:</strong> 1.12g <li><strong>Monounsaturated fat:</strong> 2.95g <li><strong>Cholesterol:</strong> 15.5mg <li><strong>Sodium:</strong> 111mg <li><strong>Potassium:</strong> 91mg <li><strong>Carbohydrates:</strong> 14.2g <li><strong>Fiber:</strong> 1.7g <li><strong>Sugar:</strong> 7.7g <li><strong>Protein:</strong> 3.8g <li><strong>Vitamin A:</strong> 22.54IU <li><strong>Calcium:</strong> 25.8mg <li><strong>Iron:</strong> 1.08mg</li></li></li></li></li></li></li></li></li></li></li></li></li></li></li></ul> </div>

<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Kathy" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/15b437d988403a18178f7b8e3ea7ded1?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/15b437d988403a18178f7b8e3ea7ded1?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Kathy" width="96"><span itemprop="name">Kathy</span> <span class="says">says</span> </img></p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/healthier-peanut-butter-chocolate-chip-cookies-gf-1-bowl/?t=1582401300#comment-864448">February 18, 2020 at 6:36 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I’ve made these twice this week (and might make them again tonight!). They come together so quick and clean up is easy. They are so delicious.  Love love love.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Just made these and YUM! My daughter is vegan so I used a little under a quarter cup of Just Egg instead of the egg in the recipe. And since I didn’t have any gluten free flour on hand, I just blended a quarter cup of the GF oats for the flour. They turned out delicious — I’m keeping this recipe for sure!</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/healthier-peanut-butter-chocolate-chip-cookies-gf-1-bowl/?t=1582401300#comment-860114">February 4, 2020 at 2:01 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I made a vegan version by replacing the egg with 1/4 cup aquafaba and they turned out perfect! I also used 1/4 cup organic cane sugar instead of 1/2 cup brown sugar and they turned sweet enough. I’m glad I didn’t add any more sugar!</p>
<p>I’m wondering though if I could replace the sugar with real maple syrup so it’s more nutritious? Thanks.</p>

<p>I made these yesterday! I substituted flax (1 tablespoon of flax meal plus 3 tablespoons of water) for the hen period. I also added 1 tablespoon of oat milk into the batter since mine seemed to be a bit dry. The cookies turned out delicious! Super peanut buttery and sweet! I will definitely make these again soon.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>So I made these last night and now I’m making them again. This time, though, I’m doubling the recipe because 4 of my kids inhaled the 12 cookies in like 3.2 nanoseconds… faster than kid #5 could get to them! These were super-easy and super-quick to make. The only change I made was using regular non-drippy peanut butter (Jif) because that’s all I had. They were perfect! Thank you, Dana, for yet another fantastic recipe!</p>

<p>What a great recipe, so easy and delicious! I usually have MB’s gluten free flour mix on hand but was out so used Bob’s Red Mill gluten free flour instead. I like crispier cookies so these stayed in the oven for an extra four minutes (I also live at a high altitude and that affects cooking time sometimes too). Just finished a second batch and saw in the recipe the addition of salt on top of the cookies when cooling…ran into the kitchen to sprinkle some Maldon sea salt flakes on the cooling cookies and am looking forward to tasting that special addition!</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-859569">
<article id="article-comment-859569">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for sunnybaby" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/3dd8097abbdec22d598b8870b7a9386b?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/3dd8097abbdec22d598b8870b7a9386b?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for sunnybaby" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">sunnybaby</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/healthier-peanut-butter-chocolate-chip-cookies-gf-1-bowl/?t=1582401300#comment-859569">February 2, 2020 at 11:25 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Appreciated the simplicity of the recipe. </p>
<p>Adaptations (based on what was available to me): 1) No peanut butter so used almond butter instead; 2) No chocolate chips, so used equal amount cocoa powder; 3) No vanilla so omitted. Did not add more sea salt on top of each cookie. Used the Minimalist Baker GF flour and otherwise followed the recipe as is. Made in a single batch, and liked it so much, I made another – this time a double batch. </p>
<p>Results:  Delivered the expected of servings. Tastes good despite the adaptations. Salty and sweet. Did not expand to double as recipe indicated, but didn’t make a difference to me.</p>
<p>Definitely keeping this one back pocket – thanks!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Loved these. Mine came out a little flat. Probably because I used local organic oats which are very tender/soft and I used homemade peanut butter. I used white whole wheat flour.  The taste was amazing, so easy to make. I used Lily chocolate chips because I had them on hand, don’t really like them much, but they were good in these cookies! These were such a hit, I made a double batch for the freezer the next day.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Yummy. This is a keeper.<br>
Different continent, different peanut butter, my cookies did not expend. I could probably press them a little more before baking then. But event with pressing them only a little, i like them a lot. Taste and look.<br>
The peanut butter i used is actually 100% peanuts (no salt). The quantity of « fleur de sel » i used for the recipe still makes it perfectly balanced to my taste. Would not add more.<br/>
If I am not mistaken, you mention (in the ingredients) salt for in the dough and somehow on top.. but I did not see it mentioned in the recipe so was wondering if you suggest to add some salt on top of the cookies as well before baking.<br/>
Thanks a lot for the metric conversion too ! Made my life soooo much easier :-)</br></br></p>

<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for whit" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/9c2e61d27dd7edb143109852e6931b70?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/9c2e61d27dd7edb143109852e6931b70?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for whit" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">whit</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/healthier-peanut-butter-chocolate-chip-cookies-gf-1-bowl/?t=1582401300#comment-859424">February 2, 2020 at 12:40 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Just made these. I have to say the raw dough tasted darn good. The cookies were quite good, but rather crumbly. I used half gf flour and half almond flour.  I think next time I would put half the amount of sugar and wouldnt add in extra salt because I think the salt from the PB was enough. But definitely a good foundation and the flavour is there!</p>

I experimented  by  adding  some dried cherries, unsweetened shredded coconut coconut sugar and more peanut butter. The cookies were even better!<br/>

a healthy treat that is dairy and gluten free.</p>

<p>Loved how quick these are to make. I reduced sugar to 1 T, subbed half the pb with pb powder, and used 2T chocolate chips. Had to add a tad more oat flour because of the pb sub, but they turned out great.</p>

<img alt="Avatar for Audrey" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/1e3475dda4b59606e8e159965a860766?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/1e3475dda4b59606e8e159965a860766?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Audrey" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Audrey</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/healthier-peanut-butter-chocolate-chip-cookies-gf-1-bowl/?t=1582401300#comment-859031">January 31, 2020 at 3:03 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I have made these twice now. First time with double the recipe size of rolled oats &amp; 1/4 Cup almond flour. I only had natural pb  without salt but found the 1/4 tsp in your regular recipe enough. Used coconut sugar instead of brown. Second time I made oat flour out of 1/2 the rolled oats and just used that with the rolled oats – same other substitutions as above. Each made about 20 small cookies and took about 14 mins to bake switching 2 cookie pans 1/2 way between top and bottom. Great reviews from family and friends each time. Thank you so much for your creative and easy recipes.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Hi, Judy! I haven’t tried these with an egg replacer. But if you try a chia egg, let us know how it goes! I’d probably recommend aquafaba instead. Check out this <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/guide-to-egg-substitutes/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Guide to Egg Substitutes</a> for details on these substitutes and more.</p>

I appreciate the notes making it customizable for you dietary needs. THANK YOU for your trial and error perfecting this cookie!</p>

Anyway, I recently went GF, so thank you for another easy recipe!</p>

				jQuery(document).ready(function () {

					function mgclInit() {
						if (jQuery.fn.off) {
							jQuery('.no-lightbox, .no-lightbox img').off('click'); // jQuery 1.7+
						}
						else {
							jQuery('.no-lightbox, .no-lightbox img').unbind('click'); // < jQuery 1.7
						}
						jQuery('a.no-lightbox').click(mgclOnClick);

						if (jQuery.fn.off) {
							jQuery('a.set-target').off('click'); // jQuery 1.7+
						}
						else {
							jQuery('a.set-target').unbind('click'); // < jQuery 1.7
						}
						jQuery('a.set-target').click(mgclOnClick);
					}

					function mgclOnClick() {
						if (!this.target || this.target == '' || this.target == '_self')
							window.location = this.href;
						else
							window.open(this.href,this.target);
						return false;
					}

					// From WP Gallery Custom Links
					// Reduce the number of  conflicting lightboxes
					function mgclAddLoadEvent(func) {
						var oldOnload = window.onload;
						if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
							window.onload = func;
						} else {
							window.onload = function() {
								oldOnload();
								func();
							}
						}
					}

					mgclAddLoadEvent(mgclInit);
					mgclInit();

				});
